1. Introduction

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 354) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 355) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 356)

This document enumerates the requirements that must be met in order for 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 357) devices to be compatible with Android ANDROID_VERSION.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 358) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 359)

The use of “MUST”, “MUST NOT”, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 360) “REQUIRED”, “SHALL”, “SHALL NOT”, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 361) “SHOULD”, “SHOULD NOT”, “RECOMMENDED”, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 362) “MAY”, and “OPTIONAL” is per the IETF standard 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 363) defined in RFC2119.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 364) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 365)

As used in this document, a “device implementer” or 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 366) “implementer” is a person or organization developing a 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 367) hardware/software solution running Android ANDROID_VERSION. A “device 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 368) implementation” or “implementation is the hardware/software solution 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 369) so developed.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 370) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 371)

To be considered compatible with Android ANDROID_VERSION, device 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 372) implementations MUST meet the requirements presented in this Compatibility 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 373) Definition, including any documents incorporated via reference.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 374) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 375)

Where this definition or the software tests described in 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 376) section 10 is silent, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 377) ambiguous, or incomplete, it is the responsibility of the device 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 378) implementer to ensure compatibility with existing implementations.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 379) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 380)

For this reason, the Android Open Source 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 381) Project is both the reference and preferred implementation of Android. 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 382) Device implementers are STRONGLY RECOMMENDED to base their implementations to 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 383) the greatest extent possible on the “upstream” source code available 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 384) from the Android Open Source Project. While some components can hypothetically 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 385) be replaced with alternate implementations, it is STRONGLY RECOMMENDED to not 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 386) follow this practice, as passing the software tests will become substantially 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 387) more difficult. It is the implementer’s responsibility to ensure full 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 388) behavioral compatibility with the standard Android implementation, including and 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 389) beyond the Compatibility Test Suite. Finally, note that certain component 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 390) substitutions and modifications are explicitly forbidden by this document.

767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 391) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 392)

Many of the resources linked to in this document are derived directly or 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 393) indirectly from the Android SDK and will be functionally identical to the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 394) information in that SDK’s documentation. In any cases where this 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 395) Compatibility Definition or the Compatibility Test Suite disagrees with the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 396) SDK documentation, the SDK documentation is considered authoritative. Any 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 397) technical details provided in the linked resources throughout this document are 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 398) considered by inclusion to be part of this Compatibility Definition.

  • Device implementers MAY modify the underlying implementation of the APIs, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1227) but such modifications MUST NOT impact the stated behavior and Java-language 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1228) signature of any publicly exposed APIs.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1229)
  • Device implementers MUST NOT add any publicly exposed elements (such as 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1230) classes or interfaces, or fields or methods to existing classes or interfaces) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1231) to the APIs above.
    • 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1232)
5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1233) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1234)

A “publicly exposed element” is any construct that is not 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1235) decorated with the“@hide” marker as used in the upstream Android 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1236) source code. In other words, device implementers MUST NOT expose new APIs or 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1237) alter existing APIs in the namespaces noted above. Device implementers MAY make 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1238) internal-only modifications, but those modifications MUST NOT be advertised or 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1239) otherwise exposed to developers.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1240) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1241)

Device implementers MAY add custom APIs, but any such APIs MUST NOT be in a 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1242) namespace owned by or referring to another organization. For instance, device 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1243) implementers MUST NOT add APIs to the com.google.* or similar namespace: only 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1244) Google may do so. Similarly, Google MUST NOT add APIs to other companies' 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1245) namespaces. Additionally, if a device implementation includes custom APIs 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1246) outside the standard Android namespace, those APIs MUST be packaged in an 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1247) Android shared library so that only apps that explicitly use them (via the 2e62f9a7 (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 23:01:44 -0700 1248) lt;uses-librarygt; mechanism) are affected by the increased memory usage of such 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1249) APIs.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1250) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1251)

If a device implementer proposes to improve one of the package namespaces 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1252) above (such as by adding useful new functionality to an existing API, or adding 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1253) a new API), the implementer SHOULD visit 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1254) source.android.com and begin the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1255) process for contributing changes and code, according to the information on that 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1256) site.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 1257) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1258)

Note that the restrictions above correspond to standard conventions for 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1259) naming APIs in the Java programming language; this section simply aims to 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1260) reinforce those conventions and make them binding through inclusion in this 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 1261) Compatibility Definition.

5.6. Audio Latency

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2777) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2778) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2779)

Audio latency is the time delay as an audio signal passes through a system. 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2780) Many classes of applications rely on short latencies, to achieve real-time 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2781) sound effects.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2782) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2783)

For the purposes of this section, use the following definitions:

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2784) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 2785)
    767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2786)
  • output latency. The interval between when an application 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2787) writes a frame of PCM-coded data and when the corresponding sound can be heard 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2788) by an external listener or observed by a transducer.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2789)
  • cold output latency. The output latency for the first 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2790) frame, when the audio output system has been idle and powered down prior to 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2791) the request.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2792)
  • continuous output latency. The output latency for 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2793) subsequent frames, after the device is playing audio.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2794)
  • input latency. The interval between when an external 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2795) sound is presented to the device and when an application reads the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2796) corresponding frame of PCM-coded data.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2797)
  • cold input latency. The sum of lost input time and the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2798) input latency for the first frame, when the audio input system has been idle 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2799) and powered down prior to the request.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2800)

    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2806)
  • continuous round-trip latency. The sum of continuous 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2807) input latency plus continuous output latency plus one buffer period. The 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2808) buffer period term allows processing time for the app and for the app to 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2809) mitigate phase difference between input and output streams.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2810)
  • OpenSL ES PCM buffer queue API. The set of PCM-related 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 2811) OpenSL ES APIs within Android NDK; see NDK_root/docs/opensles/index.html.

Android includes support for a variety of touchscreens, touch pads, and fake 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3469) touch input devices. 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3470) Touchscreen 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3471) based device implementations are associated with a display such that the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3472) user has the impression of directly manipulating items on screen. Since the user 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3473) is directly touching the screen, the system does not require any additional 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3474) affordances to indicate the objects being manipulated. In contrast, a fake touch 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3475) interface provides a user input system that approximates a subset of touchscreen 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3476) capabilities. For example, a mouse or remote control that drives an on-screen 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3477) cursor approximates touch, but requires the user to first point or focus then 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3478) click. Numerous input devices like the mouse, trackpad, gyro-based air mouse, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3479) gyro-pointer, joystick, and multi-touch trackpad can support fake touch 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3480) interactions. Android includes the feature constant android.hardware.faketouch, 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3481) which corresponds to a high-fidelity non-touch (pointer-based) input device such 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3482) as a mouse or trackpad that can adequately emulate touch-based input (including 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3483) basic gesture support), and indicates that the device supports an emulated 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3484) subset of touchscreen functionality. Device implementations that declare the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3485) fake touch feature MUST meet the fake touch requirements in 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 3486) section 7.2.5.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 3487) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 3488)

Device implementations MUST report the correct feature corresponding to the 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 3489) type of input used. Device implementations that include a touchscreen 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 3490) (single-touch or better) MUST report the platform feature constant 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 3491) android.hardware.touchscreen. 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4122) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4123) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4124)

“Telephony” as used by the Android APIs and this document refers 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4125) specifically to hardware related to placing voice calls and sending SMS messages 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4126) via a GSM or CDMA network. In other 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4129) words, the Android “telephony” functionality and APIs refer 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4130) specifically to voice calls and SMS. For instance, device implementations that 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4131) cannot place calls or send/receive SMS messages MUST NOT report the 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4132) android.hardware.telephony feature or any subfeatures, regardless of whether 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4133) they use a cellular network for data connectivity.

Android MAY be used on devices that do not include telephony hardware. That 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 4136) is, Android is compatible with devices that are not phones. However, if a device 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4137) implementation does include GSM or CDMA telephony, it MUST implement full 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4138) support for the API for that technology. 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4397) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4398) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4399)

7.5. Cameras

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4449) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4450) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4451)

Device implementations SHOULD include a rear-facing camera and MAY include a 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4452) front-facing camera. A rear-facing camera is a camera located on the side of 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4453) the device opposite the display; that is, it images scenes on the far side of 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4454) the device, like a traditional camera. A front-facing camera is a camera 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4455) located on the same side of the device as the display; that is, a camera 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4456) typically used to image the user, such as for video conferencing and similar 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 4457) applications.

9.10. Verified Boot

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5352) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5353)

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5354) Verified boot is a feature that guarantees the integrity of the device software. 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5355) If a device implementation supports the feature, it MUST: 54e6ac15 (Glenn Kasten 2015-08-12 09:07:12 -0700 5356)

    767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5358)
  • Declare the platform feature flag android.software.verified_boot.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5359)
  • Perform verification on every boot sequence.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5360)
  • Start verification from an immutable hardware key that is the root of 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5361) trust and go all the way up to the system partition.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5362)
  • Implement each stage of verification to check the integrity and 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5363) authenticity of all the bytes in the next stage before executing the code in 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5364) the next stage.
    • 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5365)
  • Use verification algorithms as strong as current recommendations from NIST 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5366) for hashing algorithms (SHA-256) and public key sizes (RSA-2048).
    • 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5367)
5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5368) 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5369)

The upstream Android Open Source Project provides a preferred implementation 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5370) of this feature based on the Linux kernel feature dm-verity.

5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5469) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5470) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5471)

Device implementations MUST pass all tests for 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5479) hardware that they possess; for instance, if a device possesses an 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5480) accelerometer, it MUST correctly execute the Accelerometer test case in the CTS 767b2721 (Heidi von Markham 2016-02-09 10:54:20 -0800 5481) Verifier. Every device and every build MUST correctly run the CTS Verifier, as noted 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5485) above. However, since many builds are very similar, device implementers are not 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5486) expected to explicitly run the CTS Verifier on builds that differ only in 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5487) trivial ways.     • 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5508)
5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5509) 5bc8114a (Unsuk Jung 2015-07-16 22:27:20 -0700 5510)
